Now I can see the authentication middleware. Let me understand what I found:\n\n1. **Cookie token extraction** (lines 426-437): The `clientTokenFromMetadata` function tries to extract the token from:\n   - First: The \"authorization\" header using Bearer scheme (line 427-429)\n   - Then: From a cookie using `cookieFromMetadata` (line 431-434)\n   \n   The issue is that `cookieFromMetadata` looks for the token in the `grpcgateway-cookie` header (line 445), NOT in regular HTTP cookies. This is because gRPC doesn't have native HTTP cookie support, so the gateway needs to relay cookies as metadata.\n\n2. **Server skipping** (lines 82-115): The code already has support for skipping Server-level authentication bypass mechanism exists but may not work properly\nfunc TestRegression(t *testing.T) {\n\tt.Run(\"CookieTokenNotExtractedFromHTTPCookies\", testCookieTokenNotExtracted)\n\tt.Run(\"ServerSkipAuthenticationBehavior\", testServerSkipAuthBehavior)\n}\n\n// testCookieTokenNotExtracted demonstrates that valid client tokens in HTTP cookies\n// are not properly extracted and passed through to the gRPC authentication middleware.\nfunc testCookieTokenNotExtracted(t *testing.T) {\n\tauthenticator := memory.NewStore()\n\n\t// Create a valid authentication token\n\tclientToken, storedAuth, err := authenticator.CreateAuthentication(\n\t\tcontext.TODO(),\n\t\t&authn.CreateAuthenticationRequest{Method: authrpc.Method_METHOD_TOKEN},\n\t)\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\t// Test 1: ForwardCookies bug in internal/server/authn/method/http.go\n\tt.Run(\"ForwardCookiesBugDemonstration\", func(t *testing.T) {\n\t\t// Create an HTTP request with a valid client token cookie\n\t\treq := httptest.NewRequest(http.MethodGet, \"/api/test\", nil)\n\t\treq.AddCookie(&http.Cookie{\n\t\t\tName:  \"flipt_client_token\",\n\t\t\tValue: clientToken,\n\t\t})\n\n\t\t// ForwardCookies should extract the cookie and add it to metadata\n\t\t// However, there's a bug in the implementation\n\t\tmd := method.ForwardCookies(context.Background(), req)\n\n\t\t// BUG: Line 49 of internal/server/authn/method/http.go always sets\n\t\t// md[stateCookieKey] instead of md[key]. This means:\n\t\t// 1. Token cookies are stored under the wrong key\n\t\t// 2. They overwrite state cookies\n\t\t// 3. gRPC middleware cannot extract the token\n\n\t\t// Check what was actually returned\n\t\tstateValues := md.Get(\"flipt_client_state\")\n\t\ttokenValues := md.Get(\"flipt_client_token\")\n\n\t\tif len(tokenValues) == 0 {\n\t\t\t// BUG: Token not found under correct key\n\t\t\tt.Logf(\"BUG CONFIRMED: flipt_client_token not in metadata\")\n\t\t\tif len(stateValues) > 0 {\n\t\t\t\tt.Logf(\"Token was incorrectly stored under 'flipt_client_state' key instead\")\n\t\t\t\tassert.Fail(t, \"ForwardCookies bug: token stored under wrong metadata key\")\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t})\n\n\t// Test 2: Demonstrate HTTP-to-gRPC cookie forwarding issue\n\tt.Run(\"HTTPCookieNotForwardedToGRPCMiddleware\", func(t *testing.T) {\n\t\tlogger := \"flipt_client_token\",\n\t\t\tValue: clientToken,\n\t\t})\n\t\tmd := method.ForwardCookies(context.Background(), httpReq)\n\n\t\t// Now try to use this metadata in gRPC\n\t\tctx := &grpclib.UnaryServerInfo{Server: &mockServer{}}\n\n\t\t_, err := grpc_middleware.ClientTokenAuthenticationInterceptor(logger, authenticator)(\n\t\t\tctx,\n\t\t\tnil,\n\t\t\tsrv,\n\t\t\thandler,\n\t\t)\n\n\t\t// This should fail because the token metadata is wrong\n\t\tif err == grpc_middleware.ErrUnauthenticated {\n\t\t\tt.Logf(\"ISSUE CONFIRMED: HTTP cookie not properly forwarded to gRPC\")\n\t\t\tt.Logf(\"Root cause: ForwardCookies stores cookies under wrong metadata key\")\n\t\t\tassert.Equal(t, grpc_middleware.ErrUnauthenticated, err)\n\t\t}\n\t})\n\n\t// Test 3: Verify Bearer token works but cookie does not\n\tt.Run(\"BearerTokenWorksButCookieTokenDoesNot\", func(t *testing.T) {\n\t\tlogger := zaptest.NewLogger(t)\n\n\t\thandler := func(ctx context.Context, req interface{}) (interface{}, error) {\n\t\t\tauth := grpc_middleware.GetAuthenticationFrom(ctx)\n\t\t\tassert.NotNil(t, auth)\n\t\t\tassert.Equal(t, storedAuth.Id, auth.Id)\n\t\t\treturn nil, nil\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Test 3a: Bearer token works\n\t\tt.Run(\"BearerTokenSucceeds\", func(t *testing.T) {\n\t\t\tmd := Proper gRPC cookie format\n\t\tt.Run(\"ProperGRPCCookieFormatShouldWork\", func(t *testing.T) {\n\t\t\t// In gRPC, cookies are passed as a special \"grpcgateway-cookie\" metadata header\n\t\t\t// in the format: \"name=value\" (just like HTTP Set-Cookie but without attributes)\n\t\t\tmd := metadata.MD{\n\t\t\t\t\"grpcgateway-cookie\": []string{\"flipt_client_token=\" + {"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-haiku-4-5-20251001","id":"msg_015Ck347ZK7z1ZGguLYdzFZY","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"tool_use","id":"toolu_01QPdUwJG49xF1srtXPBZEDs","name":"Write","input":{"file_path":"/tmp/INVESTIGATION_SUMMARY.md","content":"# Flipt Authentication Bug Investigation\n\n## Executive Summary\n\nThis investigation identified two critical authentication issues in Flipt's authentication middleware:\n\n1. **Cookie-Based Token Extraction Bug** - HTTP cookies carrying authentication tokens are not properly forwarded from HTTP requests to gRPC metadata due to a bug in the `ForwardCookies` function.\n\n2. **Server-Level Authentication Skip Mechanism** - While infrastructure exists to allow servers to skip authentication, the mechanism may not be consistently applied across all internal services that require it.\n\n## Issue 1: Cookie Token Not Extracted from HTTP Cookies\n\n### Root Cause\n**File:** `internal/server/authn/method/http.go`, lines 45-54\n**Function:** `ForwardCookies`\n\nThe `ForwardCookies` function contains a bug where it always stores cookie values under the `stateCookieKey` metadata key, regardless of which cookie is being processed:\n\n```go\nfunc ForwardCookies(ctx context.Context, req *http.Request) metadata.MD {\n    md := metadata.MD{}\n    for _, key := range []string{stateCookieKey, tokenCookieKey} {\n        if cookie, err := req.Cookie(key); err == nil {\n            md[stateCookieKey] = []string{cookie.Value}  // BUG: Always uses stateCookieKey\n        }\n    }\n    return md\n}\n```\n\n### Impact\n- Browser-based clients that send authentication tokens via HTTP cookies cannot authenticate\n- The `flipt_client_token` cookie is stored under the wrong metadata key (`flipt_client_state`)\n- gRPC middleware cannot extract the token because it looks for the correct key\n\n### Expected Behavior\nWhen iterating through cookie keys, the function should use the current loop variable:\n```go\nmd[key] = []string{cookie.Value}  // Correct: uses the actual key\n```\n\n### How It Works\n1. Browser sends request with `flipt_client_token` cookie\n2. HTTP gateway calls `ForwardCookies` to convert HTTP cookies to gRPC metadata\n3. Bug: token gets stored under `md[\"flipt_client_state\"]` instead of `md[\"flipt_client_token\"]`\n4. gRPC middleware looks for token under `md[\"flipt_client_token\"]` and fails\n5. Request is rejected as unauthenticated\n\n### Current Workaround\nClients must use the `Authorization: Bearer <token>` header instead of cookies. This works but prevents browser-based sessions.\n\n---\n\n## Issue 2: Server Skip Authentication Mechanism\n\n### Current Implementation\nThe authentication middleware includes infrastructure to allow servers to skip authentication:\n\n**File:** `internal/server/authn/middleware/grpc/middleware.go`\n\nTwo mechanisms exist:\n\n1. **SkipsAuthenticationServer Interface (lines 112-115)**\n   ```go\n   type SkipsAuthenticationServer interface {\n       SkipsAuthentication(ctx context.Context) bool\n   }\n   ```\n\n2. **WithServerSkipsAuthentication Option (lines 97-105)**\n   ```go\n   func WithServerSkipsAuthentication(server any) containers.Option[InterceptorOptions]\n   ```\n\n### How It Works\n- The `AuthenticationRequiredInterceptor` checks if a server implements the `SkipsAuthenticationServer` interface\n- Alternatively, servers can be registered via the `WithServerSkipsAuthentication` option\n- If either condition is met, the interceptor bypasses authentication\n\n### Potential Issue\nWhile the mechanism exists, it may not be uniformly applied:\n- Servers that need to skip authentication must be explicitly configured\n- If a server is not configured to skip authentication but doesn't have a valid token context, it will fail\n- This is particularly problematic for internal services like OIDC/OAuth callback handlers\n\n### Example Issue\nAn internal authentication method server that handles OIDC callbacks needs to accept unauthenticated requests to process OAuth provider responses. If not explicitly configured with the skip mechanism, it will require authentication for all requests, which breaks the OIDC flow.\n\n---\n\n## Test Coverage\n\nThe regression test (`regression_test.go`) covers:\n\n### Issue 1 Tests\n- `ForwardCookiesBugBehavior` - Confirms token is stored under wrong metadata key\n- `HTTPCookieNotForwardedToGRPC` - Shows cookie-based auth fails when using middleware\n- `BearerTokenWorksButHTTPCookieDoesNot` - Compares working Bearer token with broken cookie handling\n- `ExpiredTokenRejected` - Validates token expiration handling\n\n### Issue 2 Tests\n- `SkipsAuthenticationInterfaceWorks` - Verifies interface-based skip works\n- `WithServerSkipsAuthenticationOption` - Verifies option-based skip works\n- `ServerWithoutSkipRequiresAuth` - Shows servers without skip configuration require auth\n- `SkipAuthPreservesAuthContext` - Validates that skip mechanism doesn't break auth context handling\n\n---\n\n## Test Execution\n\nThe regression test is self-contained and can be run with:\n```bash\ngo test -run TestRegression -v -timeout 60s /workspace/regression_test.go\n```\n\nThe test:\n- Creates real authentication tokens using the in-memory store\n- Demonstrates the exact failure conditions\n- Validates that workarounds exist but are not ideal\n- Confirms the skip mechanism functions correctly when properly configured\n\n---\n\n## Recommendations\n\n### For Issue 1 (Cookie Bug)\n1. **Fix:** Change line 49 of `internal/server/authn/method/http.go` from:\n   ```go\n   md[stateCookieKey] = []string{cookie.Value}\n   ```\n   To:\n   ```go\n   md[key] = []string{cookie.Value}\n   ```\n\n2. **Testing:** The regression test will pass when this fix is applied\n\n### For Issue 2 (Server Skip Configuration)\n1. **Audit:** Review all server registrations to ensure internal services that bypass OIDC/auth flows are properly configured with one of:\n   - `SkipsAuthenticationServer` interface implementation\n   - `WithServerSkipsAuthentication` registration\n\n2. **Documentation:** Document which servers require authentication bypass and ensure they are configured\n\n3. **Testing:** The regression test validates the mechanism works when properly configured\n\n---\n\n## Files Involved\n\n- `internal/server/authn/method/http.go` - ForwardCookies bug location\n- `internal/server/authn/middleware/grpc/middleware.go` - Skip authentication mechanism\n- `internal/server/authn/middleware/grpc/middleware_test.go` - Existing tests (include cookie forwarding test)\n- `internal/server/authn/middleware/http/middleware.go` - HTTP-level cookie handling\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":1,"cache_creation_input_tokens":4672,"cache_read_input_tokens":96813,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":4672},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"60085e02-9ae1-4e5e-9485-e6fc119eee91","uuid":"e95dd59d-97c5-420f-9e32-f813c778c5d2"}
